GT: F0*sin(t) - beta*sin(x)*v - c0*beta*v - mu*(c1 - x**c2)*v - omega0**c3*x*exp(-Abs(x))
Candidates evaluated: 50

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.748007302808642*v*(1 - x**2) - 0.377828837635262*v*sin(x) - 0.755657675270524*v - 3.87049024210282*x*exp(-Abs(x)) + 0.26471389821047*sin(t)`

Let me expand this:
`0.748007302808642*v*x**2 - 0.748007302808642*v - 0.377828837635262*v*sin(x) - 0.755657675270524*v - 3.87049024210282*x*exp(-Abs(x)) + 0.26471389821047*sin(t)`

Combining v terms:
`0.748007302808642*v*x**2 - 1.503665678079166*v - 0.377828837635262*v*sin(x) - 3.87049024210282*x*exp(-Abs(x)) + 0.26471389821047*sin(t)`

The GT has these basis functions/terms:
1. `v*x**2` - v times x squared
2. `v` - linear in v
3. `v*sin(x)` - v times sin(x)
4. `x*exp(-Abs(x))` - x times exp(-|x|)
5. `sin(t)` - sine of t

Key observations:
- The term `x*exp(-|x|)` involves `Abs(x)`, which behaves differently for positive and negative x
- `v*sin(x)` is a product of v and sin(x)
- `sin(t)` is the time-dependent forcing

Now let me analyze each candidate systematically. I'll focus on whether each candidate can produce all five basis functions.

**Critical basis functions needed:**
- `v*sin(x)` — very few candidates have this
- `x*exp(-Abs(x))` — note that `x*exp(-|x|)` is NOT the same as `x*exp(cx)` for any constant c, because exp(-|x|) is not exp(cx) (it's piecewise)
- `v*x**2`
- `v`
- `sin(t)`

Let me check `x*exp(-Abs(x))`: For x>0, this is `x*exp(-x)`. For x<0, this is `x*exp(x)`. This is NOT equivalent to `x*exp(c*x)` for any single constant c, since the sign of the exponent flips.

**Candidate 1:** Has `v*x**2`, `v`, `cos(c8*t+c9)` (can match sin(t)), but no `v*sin(x)` and no `x*exp(-Abs(x))`. [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 2:** Has `x*exp(c1*x)` — not `x*exp(-|x|)`. No `v` terms. [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 3:** No `v*sin(x)`, no `x*exp(-|x|)`. [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 4-9:** None have `v*sin(x)` or `x*exp(-|x|)`. [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 10:** Has `v*x**2`, `v`, `x*exp(c1*x)`, `exp*cos` for time. Missing `v*sin(x)` and `x*exp(-|x|)` ≠ `x*exp(cx)`. [NO MATCH]

**Candidates 11-50:** I need to check each for ALL five basis functions. The critical missing ones are always `v*sin(x)` and `x*exp(-Abs(x))`.

Going through all candidates: None contain `v*sin(x)` as a term. This basis function is linearly independent from all other terms present in any candidate. Without it, no candidate can match the GT.

Additionally, `x*exp(-Abs(x))` cannot be represented by `x*exp(c*x)` since the absolute value creates a piecewise function that no single exponential can match.

Let me verify: **Candidate 30** has `v*x**2`, `v`, `cos(c5*t+c6)` (sin(t)), `x*exp(c1*x)` — still missing `v*sin(x)`.

**Candidate 17:** `v*x**2`, `v`, `x*exp(c1*x)`, `x**3`, `exp*cos` — missing `v*sin(x)`.

**Candidate 27:** `v*x**2`, `v`, `x*exp(c1*x)`, `x`, `exp*cos` — missing `v*sin(x)`.

No candidate contains `v*sin(x)`, which is required and linearly independent.
